SOV_500_days_category = {
	SOV_500_days_ticker_mission = {
		available = {
			always = no
		}
		activation = {
			has_completed_focus = SOV_capitalism_in_500_days
		}
		days_mission_timeout = 500
		is_good = no
		fire_only_once = yes
		icon = GFX_decision_gre_paying_ifc_debt
		cancel_trigger = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = SOV_500_days_ura_tt
					check_variable = { 500_days_completed = 4 }
			}
		}
		visible = {
			check_variable = { 500_days_completed < 4 }
		}

		cancel_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_500_days_ura_tt
			country_event = { id = sov_yavlinskiy.1 days = 1 }
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			country_event = { id = sov_yavlinskiy.2 days = 1 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_500_days_pizda_tt
			clr_country_flag = days_500_in_progress
		}
	}

	SOV_500_days_fase_one = {
		cost = 90
		icon = GFX_lib_button
		days_remove = 90
		fire_only_once = yes
		available = {
			check_variable = { 500_days_completed < 1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			production_speed_offices_factor = 0.07
			stability_factor = -0.05
			health_cost_multiplier_modifier = 0.05
			production_speed_buildings_factor = 0.10
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove SOV_500_days_fase_one"
			add_stability = 0.06
			set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -6 }
			modify_treasury_effect = yes
			add_to_variable = {
				var = 500_days_completed
				value = 1
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_500_days_one_tt
			add_to_variable = { SOV_500_days_offices = 0.05 }
			add_to_variable = { SOV_500_days_building = 0.05 }
			add_to_variable = { SOV_500_days_stability = 0.07 }
		}
	}

####Warsaw Pact Mechanic for USSR
###New mechanics will be added in future patches, but the core mechanics of the Warsaw Pact have been added in full
###Authors: DarkCloud, LordBogdanoff, Bondex, alexmarkel0v

SOV_restoration_of_influence_category = {
	##Poland
	SOV_influence_on_poland = {
		icon = GFX_kavkaz_revol

		cost = 25
		fire_only_once = yes
		days_remove = 20



		visible = {
			emerging_communist_state_are_in_power = yes
			NOT = { POL = {	has_autonomy_state = autonomy_warsaw } }
			POL = {
				exists = yes
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove SOV_influence_on_poland"
			POL = {
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = communism
					popularity = 0.03
				}
				recalculate_party = yes
				}
			set_country_flag = renewed_relations_with_poland
			}



		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision SOV_influence_on_poland"
			POL = {
				add_popularity = {
				ideology = communism
				popularity = 0.01
				}
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 20

			modifier = {
				factor = 20
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
	}



	SOV_perevorot = {
		icon = GFX_warsaw_button

		cost = 50
		fire_only_once = yes
		days_remove = 10

		available = {
			POL = { influence_higher_60 = yes }

		}

		visible = {
			NOT = { POL = {	has_autonomy_state = autonomy_warsaw } }
			POL = {
				exists = yes
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			POL = {
				set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 4 }
				set_temp_variable = { tag_index = SOV }
				set_temp_variable = { influence_target = POL }
				change_influence_percentage = yes
			}
			POL = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = NATO_member }
					NATO_leave = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_idea = NATO_member } }
					leave_faction = yes
				}
				add_stability = -0.06
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 } } }
					set_temp_variable = { rul_party_temp = 4 }
					change_ruling_party_effect = yes
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = communism
						elections_allowed = no
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { party_index = 4 }
				set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.45 }
				set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.45 }
				add_relative_party_popularity = yes
				set_country_flag = warsaw_member_check
			}
			SOV = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = POL
					autonomy_state = autonomy_warsaw
				}
			}
			country_event = sov_warsaw_pact.3
			set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -15 }
			modify_treasury_effect = yes
			set_country_flag = renewed_relations_with_poland4
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove SOV_perevorot"

		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 20

			modifier = {
				factor = 20
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
	}

	SOV_creation_of_faction = {
		icon = GFX_warsaw_button

		cost = 40
		fire_only_once = yes
		days_remove = 40

		available = {
			POL = {
				has_autonomy_state = autonomy_warsaw
				exists = yes
			}
		}

		visible = {
			POL = {	is_subject = yes
			has_autonomy_state = autonomy_warsaw
			}
			emerging_communist_state_are_in_power = yes
			SOV = { has_country_flag = renewed_relations_with_poland4 }
			POL = {
				exists = yes
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			POL = {
				set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 3 }
				set_temp_variable = { tag_index = SOV }
				set_temp_variable = { influence_target = POL }
				change_influence_percentage = yes
			}
			news_event = {
				hours = 1
				id = sov_warsaw_pact.2
			}
			POL = {
				country_event = sov_warsaw_pact.1
				set_country_flag = sov_northern_front
			}
			every_country = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_idea = CSTO_member
					}
					leave_faction = yes
				}
			}
			create_faction = warsaw_pact
			SOV = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = CSTO_member
					add_idea = SOV_warsaw_pact_idea
				}
			}
			POL = { add_ideas = SOV_warsaw_pact_idea }
			set_country_flag = renewed_relations_with_poland5
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove SOV_creation_of_faction"
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 20

			modifier = {
				factor = 20
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
	}

				}
				add_stability = -0.06
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 } } }
					set_temp_variable = { rul_party_temp = 4 }
					change_ruling_party_effect = yes
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = communism
						elections_allowed = no
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { party_index = 4 }
				set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.45 }
				set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.45 }
				add_relative_party_popularity = yes
				set_country_flag = warsaw_member_check
			}
			SOV = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = ROM
					autonomy_state = autonomy_warsaw
				}
			}
			ROM = { add_ideas = SOV_warsaw_pact_idea }
			country_event = sov_warsaw_pact.5
			set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -15 }
			modify_treasury_effect = yes
			set_country_flag = renewed_relations_with_romania
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove SOV_perevorot1"

		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 20

			modifier = {
				factor = 20
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
	}

					}

				set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.45 }
				set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.45 }
				add_relative_party_popularity = yes
				set_country_flag = warsaw_member_check
			}
			SOV = {
				set_autonomy = {

			}
			HUN = { add_ideas = SOV_warsaw_pact_idea }

	SOV_perevorot4 = {
		icon = GFX_warsaw_button

		cost = 50
		fire_only_once = yes
		days_remove = 10

		available = {
			AND = {
			CZE = { influence_higher_60 = yes }
			SLO = { influence_higher_60 = yes }
			}
		}

		visible = {
			NOT = { CZE = {	has_autonomy_state = autonomy_warsaw } }
			NOT = { SLO = {	has_autonomy_state = autonomy_warsaw } }
			has_country_flag = SOV_czr
			NOT = { has_country_flag = SOV_czr_close }
			AND = {
				CZE = {
					exists = yes
				}
				SLO = {
					exists = yes
				}
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			CZE = {
				set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 4 }
				set_temp_variable = { tag_index = SOV }
				set_temp_variable = { influence_target = CZE }
				change_influence_percentage = yes
			}
			news_event = {
				hours = 1
				id = sov_warsaw_pact.4
			}
			CZE = {
				country_event = sov_warsaw_pact.6
				set_country_flag = sov_northern_front
			}
			CZE = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = NATO_member }
					NATO_leave = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_idea = NATO_member } }
					leave_faction = yes
				}
				add_stability = -0.06
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 } } }
					set_temp_variable = { rul_party_temp = 4 }
					change_ruling_party_effect = yes
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = communism
						elections_allowed = no
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { party_index = 4 }
				set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.45 }
				set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.45 }
				add_relative_party_popularity = yes
				set_country_flag = warsaw_member_check
			}
			SOV = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = CZE
					autonomy_state = autonomy_warsaw
				}
			}
			SLO = {
				set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 4 }
				set_temp_variable = { tag_index = SOV }
				set_temp_variable = { influence_target = SLO }
				change_influence_percentage = yes
				set_country_flag = warsaw_member_check
			}
			news_event = {
				hours = 1
				id = sov_warsaw_pact.4
			}
			SLO = {
				country_event = sov_warsaw_pact.6
				set_country_flag = sov_northern_front
			}
			SLO = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = NATO_member }
					NATO_leave = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_idea = NATO_member } }
					leave_faction = yes
				}
				add_stability = -0.06
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 } } }
					set_temp_variable = { rul_party_temp = 4 }
					change_ruling_party_effect = yes
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = communism
						elections_allowed = no
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { party_index = 4 }
				set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.45 }
				set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.45 }
				add_relative_party_popularity = yes
			}
			SOV = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = SLO
					autonomy_state = autonomy_warsaw
				}
			}
			country_event = sov_warsaw_pact.5

			modify_treasury_effect = yes
			set_country_flag = first_step_of_czr
